  <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>The benefit of threading that most sets it apart from other hair removal techniques is its precision. While waxing and plucking can often leave unwanted stray hairs around your eyebrows, a threading artist goes through your hair row by row, giving eyebrows a clean and defined shape. Threading only removes hair, not skin, and because it is so exact, it can remove hairs that are finer than those that can be removed by waxing or plucking. Threading is an ancient method of hair removal practiced by the people of South Asia and Arabia. It is a delicate procedure and involves hair removal with the means of highly skilled hands using special thread to pluck and pull hair out from the roots. One of the greatest benefits of threading is that it is less messy and faster as compared to waxing or tweezing for hair removal purposes. Especially hair on the upper lip and eyebrows. Waxing causes redness and irritation. With threading no matter how sensitive your skin is you will never get that extreme redness, soreness and sometimes scarring caused by pulling out the follicle of your eyebrow hairs by waxing. If the temperature of the wax is not exactly right than that too can cause severe irritation.<span class="more-links"><a title="Read More about Signature Eyebrows Threading Salon" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDesc(this)">Read more</a></span></p>

    <p>Traditional Henna by Karen, I specialize in traditional designs from Middle East, Africa, and India. I have been doing henna for over 15 years which allows me to draw quickly, when doing henna at events and parties. I enjoy free-styling designs. I mix my own natural henna paste by hand and use only the finest ingredients. My henna interest in henna started when I first had henna done on me in the early 90''s. Since that first time, I became completely intrigued. I spent 6 months learning how to mix and apply henna, and then years of experience training in design and composition. I have grow into a full time business doing henna at events, parties, fairs, farmers'' markets, and private appointments. Henna has been my passion and I have been doing henna professionally for over a decade.  Although it has become quite commercialized, I am committed to doing traditional designs from Africa, Middle East, and India. Henna has been around for centuries, and was never intended to be a "temporary tattoo".  Each country and region has its'' own unique style.  From bold floral patterns in the Middle East and East Africa, lacey intricate Indian, to geometric designs of North and West Africa. Henna is all natural, painless, and temporary. It lasts for one week on the upper body and close to three weeks on the feet .  Once the paste has set completely, the stain on skin will turn terracotta red on light complexion, and deep burgundy on darker skin.  Many cultures believe that henna is a blessed substance.  I enjoy bringing this ancient art form to the general public.
